Question:
‡¶Ö‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï [math]\vec{A}=2 \hat{i}+\hat{j}-\widehat{k},[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\vec{B}=\widehat{i}-2 \hat{j}-3 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡ß¨‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá, ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ü ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π ‡ßü‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. [math]\vec{A}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\vec{B}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}-\hat{\mathrm{k}}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\rm{\overrightarrow{B}=\hat{i}-2 \hat{j}-3 \hat{k}}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø, [math]\overrightarrow{\rm{A}}\text{ ‡¶ì }\overrightarrow{\rm{B}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ [math]=|\overrightarrow{\rm{A}}\times\overrightarrow{\rm{B}}|[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{aligned} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}} & =\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ 2 & 1 & -1 \\ 1 & -2 & -3 \end{array}\right| \\ & =\hat{\mathrm{i}}(-3-2)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}(-6+1)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}(-4-1) \\ & =-5 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+5 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-5 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore|\overrightarrow{\rm{A}}\times\overrightarrow{\rm{B}}|=\sqrt{(-5)^{2}+5^{2}+(-5)^{2}}=5 \sqrt{3}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ [math]5 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ï‡•§

Explanation:
‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ = [math]|\vec{A}\times\vec{B}|[/math]. ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\vec{A}\times\vec{B}=\begin{vmatrix}\hat{i}&\hat{j}&\hat{k}\\2&1&-1\\1&-2&-3\end{vmatrix}=-5\hat{i}+5\hat{j}-5\hat{k}[/math], ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø [math]|\vec{A}\times\vec{B}|=5\sqrt{1+1+1}=5\sqrt{3}[/math].

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\rm{\overrightarrow{P}=3\overrightarrow{A}}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\rm{\overrightarrow {Q}=\dfrac{1}{2} \overrightarrow{B}}[/math]‡•§

[Image]


Options:
‡¶ó. [math]\rm{\overrightarrow{A}}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\rm{\overrightarrow{B}}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\qquad\begin{array}{l} \rm{\overrightarrow{A}}=2 \hat{\rm{i}}+\sqrt{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\sqrt{3} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}=\sqrt{3} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-2 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£, [math]\theta = ?[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\qquad \qquad\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}=\mathrm{AB} \cos \theta \\ \Rightarrow \cos \theta=\dfrac{\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}}{\mathrm{AB}}\\ \qquad =\dfrac{(2 \hat{\rm{i}}+\sqrt{2} \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\sqrt{3} \hat{\rm{k}}) \cdot(\sqrt{3} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-2 \hat{\mathrm{k}})}{\sqrt{2^{2}+(\sqrt{2})^{2}+(-\sqrt{3})^{2}} \times \sqrt{(\sqrt{3})^{2}+3^{2}+(-2)^{2}}} \\ \qquad =\dfrac{2 \sqrt{3}+3 \sqrt{2}+2 \sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{9} \times \sqrt{16}} \\ \qquad =\left(\dfrac{3 \sqrt{2}+4 \sqrt{3}}{12}\right)\\ \therefore ~\theta=\cos ^{-1}\left(\dfrac{3 \sqrt{2}+4 \sqrt{3}}{12}\right)=21.424^{\circ} \textbf { (Ans.) } \end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ [math]\overrightarrow{P}=3\overrightarrow{A}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{Q}=\tfrac{1}{2}\overrightarrow{B}[/math], ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{P}‚Äñ\overrightarrow{A}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{Q}‚Äñ\overrightarrow{B}[/math]‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á [math]\overrightarrow{A}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{B}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]\overrightarrow{P}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{Q}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board

Question:
‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì:

[Image]


Options:
‡¶ó. [math]\angle \mathrm{BAC}[/math] ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\rm{A(2-3,4), ~B(1,2,-5)}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\mathrm{C}(3,3,-2)[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{array}{l} \therefore \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}=\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}-\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}} \\ \qquad =(\hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-5 \hat{\mathrm{k}})-(2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+4 \hat{\mathrm{k}}) \\ \qquad =-\hat{\mathrm{i}}+5 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-9 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç[math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{aligned} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AC}}=\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OC}}-\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}} & =(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-2 \hat{\mathrm{k}})-(2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+4 \hat{\mathrm{k}}) \\ & =(\hat{\mathrm{i}}+6 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-6 \hat{\mathrm{k}}) \end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\hspace{1.1 cm}\begin{aligned} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AC}} & =|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AC}}| \cdot \cos \angle \mathrm{BAC} \\ \Rightarrow \cos \angle \mathrm{BAC} & =\frac{\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AC}}}{|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AC}}|} \\ & =\frac{(-\hat{\mathrm{i}}+5 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-\ddot{9} \hat{\mathrm{k}}) \cdot(\hat{\mathrm{i}}+6 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-6 \hat{\mathrm{k}})}{\sqrt{107} \cdot \sqrt{73}} \\ & =\frac{-1+30+54}{\sqrt{107} \times \sqrt{73}} \\ & =\frac{83}{\sqrt{107} \times \sqrt{73}} \\ \therefore \angle \mathrm{BAC}&=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{83}{\sqrt{107} \times \sqrt{73}}\right)=20.09^{\circ}(\text { Ans. }) \end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ó ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ; [math]\angle BAC[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø/‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£, ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ, ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶®‡•§

Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board

Question:

Options:
‡¶ò. [math]\rm{\triangle A O B}[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ-‡¶®‡¶æ ‚Äî ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶ì‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ò‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}=\rm{3 \hat{i}+2 \hat{j}+\hat{k}} \\ \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}=\rm{3 \hat{i}+2 \hat{j}-3 \hat{k}}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1 cm}\rm{A}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï [math]( 3, 2, 1 )[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1 cm}\rm{B}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï [math](3, 2, -3)[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1 cm}\rm{A ~‡¶ì~ B}[/math]
 ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞, [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}=\text { ? }[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{aligned} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}~ & =\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}-\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}} \\ & =(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{k}}) \rm{-(3 \hat{i}+2 \hat{j}+\hat{k})}\\ & =-4 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ |\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}| & =\sqrt{(-4)^{2}}=4 \\ |\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}| & =\sqrt{(3)^{2}+(2)^{2}+(1)^{2}}=\sqrt{14} \\ |\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}| & =\sqrt{(3)^{2}+(2)^{2}+(-3)^{2}}=\sqrt{22} \end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1 cm}\begin{array}{l} |\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}|^{2}=(\sqrt{22})^{2}=22 \\ |\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}|^{2}+|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}|^{2}=(\sqrt{14})^{2}+(4)^{2}=30 \end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, [math]|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}|^{2} 
eq|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}|^{2}+|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}|^{2}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º [math]|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}|^{2} 
eq|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}|^{2}+|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}|^{2}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{AB}}|^{2} 
eq|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}|^{2}+|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}|^{2}[/math]
‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶è‡¶¨, ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ [math]\triangle \mathrm{AOB}[/math]
 ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

‡¶ò ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å ‚Äî [math]\triangle AOB[/math] ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßÄ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø [math]\vec{OA}\cdot\vec{OB}=0[/math] ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé OA ‡¶ì OB ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø A ‡¶ì B-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶ï ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá [math](x_1,y_1)[/math] ‡¶ì [math](x_2,y_2)[/math], ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá [math]x_1x_2+y_1y_2=0[/math] ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø [math]90^\circ[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßÄ‡•§

Question #71 (ID: 397527)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board

Question:

[Image]


Options:
‡¶ó. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá [math]\rm{\angle A O B}[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, [math]\mathrm{O}(0,0,0), \mathrm{A}(3,2,1)[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\mathrm{B}(3,2,-3)[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\therefore \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}=(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}})^{\prime}[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}=(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{k}})[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\hspace{1.1 cm}\begin{aligned} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}} & =|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OA}}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OB}}| \cdot \cos \angle \mathrm{AOB}\\ \Rightarrow \cos \angle \rm{A O B} & =\rm{\frac{\overrightarrow{O A} \cdot \overrightarrow{O B}}{|\overrightarrow{O A}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{O B}|}} \\ & =\frac{(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}}) \cdot(3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}-3 \hat{\mathrm{k}})}{\sqrt{3^{2}+2^{2}+1^{2}} \cdot \sqrt{3^{2}+2^{2}+(-3)^{2}}} \\ & =\left(\frac{9 \cdot+4-3}{\sqrt{14} \cdot \sqrt{22}}\right)=\frac{10}{2 \sqrt{77}}=\frac{5}{\sqrt{77}}\\ \rm{\therefore \angle A O B} & =\cos ^{-1} \frac{5}{\sqrt{77}}=55.264^{\circ} \textbf { (Ans.) } \end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶É‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‚Äî ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ A, B ‡¶ì O ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£/‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø) ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá [math]\angle AOB[/math] ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨‡•§

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2021 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\rm{\overrightarrow{A}=2 \hat{i}+4 \hat{j}+2 \hat{k}, \overrightarrow{B}=3 \hat{i}+3 \hat{j}+4 \hat{k}}[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\rm{\overrightarrow{C}=\hat{i}+2 \hat{j}+\hat{k}}[/math]

[Image]


Options:
‡¶ó. [math]\overrightarrow{\rm{B}}\text{ ‡¶ì } \overrightarrow{\rm{A}}[/math] ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\hspace{1 cm}\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}=3 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+3 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+4 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]\hspace{1 cm}[/math]
‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤, [math]|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}|=?[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\hspace{1.5 cm}\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ 3 & 3 & 4 \\ 2 & 4 & 2 \end{array}\right| \\ \qquad =\hat{\mathrm{i}}(6-16)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}(6-8)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}(12-6) \\ \qquad =-10 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \hat{\mathrm{j}}+6 \hat{\mathrm{k}} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore ~\overrightarrow{\rm{B}}\text{ ‡¶ì }\overrightarrow{\rm{A}}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤, [math]\rm{|\overrightarrow{B} \times \overrightarrow{A}|}=\sqrt{(-1,0)^{2}+(2)^{2}+(6)^{2}}=11.83[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ï [math]\text{(Ans.)}[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{A}\times\overrightarrow{B}=10\hat{i}-2\hat{j}-6\hat{k}[/math] ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ = [math]\sqrt{10^2+(-2)^2+(-6)^2}=\sqrt{140}=2\sqrt{35}[/math]‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l} \left|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1}\right|=4 \mathrm{~N} \\ \theta_{1}=60^{\circ} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨-‡¶™‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï x ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ì ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞-‡¶¶‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï y ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1}=\left|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1}\right| \cos \theta_{1} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\left|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1}\right| \sin \theta_{1} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\ \Rightarrow \vec{F}_{1}=4 \cos 60^{\circ} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 \sin 60^{\circ} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\ \therefore \vec{F}_{1}=2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+2 \sqrt{3} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\ \vec{F}_{2}=\left|\vec{F}_{2}\right| \cos \theta(-\hat{\mathrm{i}})+\left|\vec{F}_{2}\right| \sin \theta \hat{j} \\ =-4 \cos 60^{\circ} \hat{\mathrm{i}}+4 \sin 60^{\circ} \hat{\mathrm{j}} \\ =-2 \hat{i}+2 \sqrt{3} \hat{j} \end{array}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{2}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá, x ‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ã‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£[math]\begin{aligned} \theta & =90^{\circ}-\theta_{2} \\ & =90^{\circ}-30^{\circ} \\ & =60^{\circ} \\ \left|\vec{F}_{2}\right| & =4 \mathrm{~N} \end{aligned}[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{2}[/math]
 ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º 1‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ 2‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá,[math]\begin{aligned} \left|\vec{F}_{1} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{2}\right| & =\left|\begin{array}{ccc} \hat{\mathrm{i}} & \hat{\mathrm{j}} & \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ 2 & 2 \sqrt{3} & 0 \\ -7 & 2 a \sqrt{3} & 0 \end{array}\right| \\ & =\mathrm{i}(0-0)-\hat{\mathrm{j}}(0-0)+\hat{\mathrm{k}}(4 \sqrt{3} +4 \sqrt{3})\\ & =8 \sqrt{3} \hat{\mathrm{k}} \\ \left|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{1} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{F}}_{2}\right| & =\sqrt{(8 \sqrt{3})^{2}}=8 \sqrt{3}=13.8564 \end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ = 13.8564 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ï (Ans. )

Explanation:
‡¶ó ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ = ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø √ó ‡¶â‡¶Å‡¶ö‡ßÅ = [math]|\vec F_{1}| (|\vec F_{2}|\sin\theta) = |\vec F_{1}||\vec F_{2}|\sin\theta[/math], ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\theta[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£; ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‚Äë‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ì‡•§ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶§‡¶≤‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø [math]A=|F_{1x}F_{2y}-F_{1y}F_{2x}|[/math]‡•§

Question:
‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá P (1, 2, 1) ‡¶ì Q (2, 1, 1)‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá [math]\overrightarrow{OP}[/math] ‡¶ì [math]\overrightarrow{OQ}[/math]‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡ßÅ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá R ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï R (1, 1, 2) ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. [math]\alpha[/math] ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, O(0, 0, 0), P (1, 2, 1) ‡¶ì Q (2, 1, 1).[math]\therefore \overrightarrow{O P}=(\hat{i}+2 \hat{j}+\hat{k})[/math]
 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç [math]\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OQ}}=(2 \hat{\mathrm{i}}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}})[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\begin{array}{l} \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OQ}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OP}}=|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OQ}}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OP}}| \cdot \cos \angle \mathrm{POQ} \\ \Rightarrow \cos \angle \mathrm{POQ}=\frac{\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OP}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{OQ}}}{|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OP}}| \cdot|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{OQ}}|} \\ =\frac{(\hat{i}+2 \hat{j}+\hat{k}) \cdot(2 \hat{i}+\hat{\mathrm{j}}+\hat{\mathrm{k}})}{\sqrt{1^{2}+2^{2}+1^{2}} \cdot \sqrt{2^{2}+1^{2}+1^{2}}} \\ =\left(\frac{2+2+1}{\sqrt{6} \cdot \sqrt{6}}\right)=\frac{5}{6} \\ \therefore \angle \mathrm{POQ}=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{5}{6}\right)=33.56^{\circ} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore ~ \alpha[/math]
 ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® 33.56¬∞ (Ans.)

Explanation:
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶ó [math]\overrightarrow{OP}=(1,2,1),\ \overrightarrow{OQ}=(2,1,1)[/math] ‡•§ ‡¶°‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü [math]=1\cdot2+2\cdot1+1\cdot1=5[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø [math]=\sqrt{6}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡ßü [math]\cos\alpha=\dfrac{5}{\sqrt{6}\sqrt{6}}=\dfrac{5}{6}[/math] ‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá [math]\alpha=\cos^{-1}\!\big(\tfrac{5}{6}\big)\approx 33.56^\circ[/math] ‡•§

 ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø R ‡•§ ‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø R ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø P ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá [math]\theta[/math]
 ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá,[math]\tan \theta=\frac{Q \sin \alpha}{P+Q \cos \alpha}[/math]
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá P = Q[math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \tan \theta=\frac{Q \sin \alpha}{Q+Q \cos \alpha}\\\text{ } \operatorname{ai} \theta=\frac{Q \sin \alpha}{Q(1+\cos \alpha)}=\frac{\sin \alpha}{1+\cos \alpha}\\\quad=\frac{2 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha}{2}}{2 \cos \frac{\alpha}{2}}=\frac{\sin \frac{\alpha}{2}}{\cos \frac{\alpha}{2}} \\\therefore \tan \theta=\tan \frac{\alpha}{2}\\\theta=\frac{a}{2}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ç, ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶£‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡•§ [math]\\[/math]

‡¶ó ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® [math]F[/math] ‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£ [math]\alpha[/math] ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞)‡¶ï‡ßá x‚Äë‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ x‚Äë‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá [math]F\cos(\alpha/2)[/math] ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç y‚Äë‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ¬±[math]F\sin(\alpha/2)[/math]; y‚Äë‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ x‚Äë‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü [math]2F\cos(\alpha/2)[/math], ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶£‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶£‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Question #76 (ID: 397523)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: ‡¶™‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶® ‡ßß‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\vec{A}=\hat{i}+\hat{j}-\hat{k} , \vec{B}=2 \hat{i}-2 \hat{j}-3 \hat{k}[/math] ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡•§

Options:
‡¶ó. ‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÄ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ö‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã ‡•§


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
‡¶ó‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞ [math]\vec{A}[/math]
 ‡¶ì [math]\vec{B}[/math]
 ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ö‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ [math]\Delta[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá,[math]\begin{array}{l}\vec{A}=\hat{i}+\hat{j}-\hat{k} \\\vec{B}=2 \hat{i}-2 \hat{j}-3 \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø,[math]\Delta=|\vec{A} \times \vec{B}|[/math]
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®,[math]\begin{array}{l}\vec{A} \times \vec{B}=\left|\begin{array}{ccc}\hat{i} & \hat{j} & \hat{k} \\1 & 1 & -1 \\2 & -2 & -3\end{array}\right| \\\Rightarrow\text { } \vec{A} \times \vec{B}=(-3-2) \hat{i}-(-3+2) \hat{j}+(-2-2) \hat{k} \\\Rightarrow\text { } \vec{A} \times \vec{B}=-5 \hat{i}+\hat{j}-4 \hat{k}\end{array}[/math]
‡¶ö‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤,[math]\begin{aligned}\Delta & =|\overrightarrow{\mathrm{A}} \times \overrightarrow{\mathrm{B}}| \\ =\sqrt{(-5)^{2}+1^{2}+(-4)^{2}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{42}[/math]
 ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ó ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ï [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé [math]\text{Area}=|\vec{A}\times\vec{B}|[/math]. ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá [math]\vec{A}\times\vec{B}=(-5)\hat{i}+1\hat{j}-4\hat{k}[/math] ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤ [math]\sqrt{(-5)^2+1^2+(-4)^2}=\sqrt{42}[/math]‡•§

Sub-Questions:
